
1.1(1): bon nyid kyi snying po bdal pa'i 
1.2(1): 'bum bzhugs so/ /
1.3(1): @#/  /bon nyid kyi snying po bdal pa'i 'bum las/ dum bu lnga pa bam po dang 
1.4(1): po'o/ /de nas seng ge zab mos gsol pa/ gnyis ka ma yin pa'i gzungs sngags 
1.5(1): kyi spyi don ci la 'dus pa lags/ gshen rab kyis bka' stsal pa/ de ni 'di lta ste/
1.6(1): gnyis ka ma yin pa'i gzungs kyi spyi rgyud khri la bsdus pa de ni/ gzungs kyi rgyud chen 
1.7(1): po nyi shu ste/
1.8(1): de gang zhe na/ yum chen mo thugs rje byams ma snying rje bskyed pa gzungs kyi rgyud 
1.9(1): dang / ma cig 'gying ma 'od mtsho spyan stong mnga' ba'i gzungs kyi rgyud dang / yi ge 
1.10(1): brgya pa dpa' bo 'bru lnga gzungs kyi rgyud dang / seng ge sgra 'byin thams cad rgyal 
1.11(1): bar byed pa gzungs kyi rgyud dang /
1.12(1): 7 de nas ston pa gshen rab mi bo la/ rigs kyi bde bar gshegs pa zhi khro 
1.13(1): bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / lha dang lha mo'i rigs bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i nang 
1.14(1): nas/ gshen rab g.yung drung sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po seng ge zab mos 
1.15(1): gsol pa/ gshen rab dpa' bo thams cad 'dren pa'i dpal/ gong du sngags kyi 
1.16(1): 'bum zhes bya ba gang lags/ / 'khor la bshad du gsol/ dpa' bo mchog gis 
1.17(1): bka' stsal pa/ sngags kyi 'bum zhes bya ba yang lus sems lha ru bsgrub pa'i phyir/
2.1(1): yang dag don la bsngags pa yin/ de la sngags 'bum de la yang sngags te/ gong 
2.2(1): khal spyir khyab pa dang bdun yin te/ de gang zhe na/ phyi rigs sngags dang / nang 
2.3(1): gsang sngags dang / gnyis ka ma yin pa'i gzungs sngags dang / drag po'i ngan 
2.4(1): sngags dang / thugs rje'i rgyun sngags dang / zhang zhung this sngags dang / bdud rtsi 
2.5(1): sman gyi gong khal dang bdun no/ /phyi rigs sngags la rgyud khri/ nang gsang sngags 
2.6(1): la rgyud bzhi khri/ gnyis ka ma yin pa'i gzungs sngags la rgyud khri/ drag po'i ngan 
2.7(1): sngags la rgyud khri/ thugs rje rgyud sngags kyi rgyud khri/ zhang zhung this sngags kyi rgyud khri/
2.8(1): bdud rtsi sman gyi rgyud khri dang 'bum ste/ sngags kyi 'bum zhes bya'o/ /zhes gsungs 
2.9(1): so/  /
2.10(1): 7 gsol pa/ phyi rigs sngags kyi rgyud khri po de dag bsdus na nges pa'i rtsa rgyud 
2.11(1): du zhig mchis/ ston mchog dpa' bos bka' stsal pa/ seng ge zab mo la sogs te/
2.12(1): phyi nang 'khor rnams nga la nyon/ phyi yi rigs sngags bya ba ni/ g.yung drung 'khor lo 
2.13(1): pad ma rin po che yi rigs bzhi'i zhing khams dang gzhal yas su chas pas/ sku dang

393.12(1): gang du bsdur ba/ bsdur ba'i legs cha gang zhig thon pa sogs glegs bam so so'i nang 
393.13(1): dang mjug gi zhus bsgrigs gsal bshad du bris yod/ mdor na nged las mi yongs 
393.14(1): kyis spyi lo 2011lo nas bzung mi lo lnga yi ring dad pa dag snang dang rang gi dge sbyor 
393.15(1): dang bstan la zhabs phyi gtso bzung thog deb rer tshar grangs bco lnga nas nyi shu bar 
393.16(1): zhus dag byas yod pas sngar las lhag pa'i legs cha zhig thon yod pa'i re ba yod/ 'on 
393.17(1): kyang re 'ga' ma dpe gcig ma gtogs bsdur ya ma rnyed pa dang / re 'ga' bsdur ya 
393.18(1): du ma rnyed kyang bris pa'i chad lhag sogs kyis gcig mtshungs med pa dang / nged zhus 
393.19(1): sgrig pa tsho'i mkhyen dpyod tshad brgal can min pa bcas dang rjes 'gro byas pas nor 
393.20(1): 'khrul gyis bslad pa'ang yod nges pas/ rjes gzigs mkhan rnam pas su dang gang la 
393.21(1): khag dkri med pa rang bstan rang skyong gi 'gan 'khri gtsang ma phrag tu khur ste bstan pa 
393.22(1): rin po che'i ched du nor 'khrul yo bsrang dag ther gnang ba'i skul ma zhu rgyu dang /

394.2(1): gis las don rlabs chen 'di 'dra zhig legs grub byung ba ni/ rig gzhung 'di dang 
394.3(1): bstan pa 'di la lhag bsam can gyis phyar gru mnyam 'degs byas pa las byung ba 
394.4(1): yin/ kan su'u mi rigs dpe skrun khang gi dbu khrid 'brug rgyal mkhar dang gcod pa 
394.5(1): rnam gnyis nas thugs khur rgyab skyor tshad med gnang ba dang / lhag par du dus rab 
394.6(1): kyi gnyan 'phrang mang po'i nang tshe srog 'ben dang bsdos te srung skyong byas pa'i dpe cha 
394.7(1): g.yar ba'i dpe bdag rnam pa dang / de bzhin nga tsho'i bstan don gyi bya ba kun la 
394.8(1): mthun sbyor gnang ba ma tshad dpe tshogs 'di dpar skrun skabs su yang ma bskul dang 
394.9(1): blang gis zhal 'debs gnang mkhan bcas dngos shugs brgyud gsum nas rgyu tshegs 
394.10(1): thabs gsum gyis sdong grogs rogs ram gnang mkhan yongs la snying dbus nas 
394.11(1): thugs rje che zhu rgyu dang / gsung rab dag bzhengs byas pa'i dge ba'i tshogs 'dis/
394.12(1): 7 skyabs rje rgyal ba sman ri ba'i mkhan slob rnam gnyis gtsos ris su ma chad pa'i 
394.13(1): bstan 'dzin skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi sku tshe bskal brgyar brtan zhing bzhed dgongs 
394.14(1): lhun gyis 'grub pa dang / 'brel thogs kyi sbyin pa'i bdag po dang las gzhi 'di'i byed 
394.15(1): po kun tshe bsod dbang khams gong nas gong du mtho ste myur du sku gsum rdzogs pa'i 
394.16(1): sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang thob pa dang / zhang bod rig gzhung rnams mi nyams gong nas 
394.17(1): gong du 'phel te 'dzam gling tha gru yongs kyi snod bcud rgud pa gso zhing phan bde'i 
394.18(1): gsos su khyab pa dang / yangs pa'i rgyal khams kun du nad mug 'khrug rtsod dang rang 
394.19(1): byung 'byung ba'i 'jigs pa rnams rmeng med du zhi nas bde legs phun tshogs skyid kyi nyi
